\se2 ɦoɔ̄isʌnɛ
\ge reveal a secret
\gn कुरा खुस्काउनु, कुरा खुलाउनु

\lx mimt
\a imt
\ps vt
\ge remember, think
\gn सोच्नु
\1e mʌ̄mdu
\a mʌm
\1d mimi
\xv ʔʌ̄mʔɛ ʦɛ̂mɦɵːtɛ̂m brâː mʌ̂mkhʌtɛ.
\xn बिर्सेको कुरा सम्झ्यो ।
\xe He remembered the things he had forgotten.
\xv ʔuŋʌ ʔʌjɛʦhɛ mʌ̂mtʌ.
\xn मैले प्रेमिकालाई सम्झें ।
\xe I remembered my lover.
\xv ɦēːsʌ kɛ̄m mʉnɛ? mʌ̄mdu ɦe muŋʌ.
\xn कसरी काम गर्ने? सोची रहेको छु ।
\xe I am thinking how to do the work.
\xv jɛʦhɛʔɛ mʌ̂mtɛkhi, ɦidimɛ mʌttɛ.
\xn मायालुले संझ्यो कि बाडुली लाग्‍यो ।
\xe As his lover remembered him, he got a hiccup.
\se mimt-si
\wav vr-mimt-si
\wav vr-mimt-si2
\ps vr
\1s mʌ̄msiŋʌ
\1d mīmsiji
\xv ʦɵʦʦɵ muŋʌtʌlo bhʌ̄ŋte ʦēiwʌsukho nōːwɛ rʌ̄iʦhʌ mʌ̄msiŋʌ.
\xn सानो छँदा राम्ररी सिकेको भए राम्रो हुन्थेछ भनेर सम्झन्छु ।
\xe I thought that it would have been good to learn well while I was a child.
\nq revise eng
\dt 07/Jul/2014

\xv ʦɵʦʦɵpo ŋʌlu ɦʌllei ʦhûː jo ʔʌ̄lkinʌkho nuri ŋʌlu bʌ̄ŋpɛ lʌ̄m.
\xn केटाकेटीको दाँत हल्लिने बित्तिकै उखालेमा नयाँ दाँत राम्रो उम्रिन्छ ।
\xe If we take out the children teeth when they shake, the new teeth grow well.
\xv sʌ̄ŋbi thânpɛ kaʈi ʣʌmʌrʌʔɛ ʔʌ̄lnɛ mʌttʉ.
\xn काठमा ठोकेको काँटी जमराले उखाल्नु पर्छ ।
\xe We have to take out the nails that have been nailed into the wood with a hammer.
\nq revoir husang + jamara
